\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{field\-\_\-offset}

\begin{DoxyCode}
{
    struct aggr aggr;
    if (num_records == 0) {
        aggr.num_values = 0;
        aggr.values = NULL;
        return aggr;
    }
    int i;
    aggr.num_values = 1;
    aggr.values = (uint64_t *)malloc(sizeof(uint64_t)*aggr.num_values);
    if (aggr.values == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    for (i = 0; i < num_records; i++) {
        aggr.values[0] &= *(uint16_t *)(records[i] + field_offset);
    }
    return aggr;
}

    struct aggr aggr;
    if (num_records == 0) {
        aggr.num_values = 0;
        aggr.values = NULL;
        return aggr;
    }
    aggr.num_values = 1;
    aggr.values = (uint64_t *)malloc(sizeof(uint64_t)*aggr.num_values);
    if (aggr.values == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    aggr.values[0] = num_records;
    return aggr;
}
\end{DoxyCode}

\subsubsection[{aggr\-\_\-median\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}struct {\bf aggr} {\bf aggr\-\_\-median\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t} (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{char $\ast$$\ast$}]{records, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{num\-\_\-records, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{field\-\_\-offset}

\begin{DoxyCode}
{
    struct aggr aggr;
    if (num_records == 0) {
        aggr.num_values = 0;
        aggr.values = NULL;
        return aggr;
    }
    int i;
    uint64_t *temp;
    temp = (uint64_t *)malloc(sizeof(uint64_t)*num_records);
    if (temp == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    for (i=0; i < num_records; i++) {
        temp[i] = *(uint16_t *)(records[i] + field_offset);
    }
    qsort(temp, num_records, sizeof(uint64_t), compar);
    aggr.num_values = 1;
    aggr.values = (uint64_t *)malloc(sizeof(uint64_t)*aggr.num_values);
    if (aggr.values == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    aggr.values[0] = temp[num_records/2];    free(temp);
    return aggr;
}

\subsubsection[{aggr\-\_\-min\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}struct {\bf aggr} {\bf aggr\-\_\-min\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t} (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{num\-\_\-records, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{field\-\_\-offset}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily  \mbox{[}read\mbox{]}}}}\label{auto__comps_8c_a76c404cda1036d373012de4f149c805a}

\begin{DoxyCode}
{
    struct aggr aggr;
    if (num_records == 0) {
        aggr.num_values = 0;
        aggr.values = NULL;
        return aggr;
    }
    int i;
    aggr.num_values = 1;
    aggr.values = (uint64_t *)malloc(sizeof(uint64_t)*aggr.num_values);
    if (aggr.values == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    aggr.values[0] = *(uint16_t *)(records[0] + field_offset);
    for (i = 1; i < num_records; i++) {
        if (*(uint16_t *)(records[0] + field_offset) < aggr.values[0]) {
            aggr.values[0] = *(uint16_t *)(records[0] + field_offset);
        }
    }
    return aggr;
}

\hypertarget{auto__comps_8c_af89f25325447c8fbb7ebddf18c190c94}{\index{auto\-\_\-comps.\-c@{auto\-\_\-comps.\-c}!aggr\-\_\-stddev\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t@{aggr\-\_\-stddev\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t}}
\index{aggr\-\_\-stddev\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t@{aggr\-\_\-stddev\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t}!auto_comps.c@{auto\-\_\-comps.\-c}}
\subsubsection[{aggr\-\_\-stddev\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}struct {\bf aggr} {\bf aggr\-\_\-stddev\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t} (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{char $\ast$$\ast$}]{records, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{num\-\_\-records, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{field\-\_\-offset}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily  \mbox{[}read\mbox{]}}}}\label{auto__comps_8c_af89f25325447c8fbb7ebddf18c190c94}

\begin{DoxyCode}
{
    struct aggr aggr;
    if (num_records == 0) {
        aggr.num_values = 0;
        aggr.values = NULL;
        return aggr;
    }
    int i;
    uint64_t stddev;
    aggr.num_values = 1;
    aggr.values = (uint64_t *)malloc(sizeof(uint64_t)*aggr.num_values);
    if (aggr.values == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    for (i = 0; i < num_records; i++) {
        aggr.values[0] += *(uint16_t *)(records[i] + field_offset);
    }
    aggr.values[0] /= num_records;
    for (i = 0; i < num_records; i++) {
        stddev += (*(uint16_t *)(records[i] + field_offset)-aggr.values[0])*(*(
      uint16_t *)(records[i] + field_offset)-aggr.values[0]);
    }
    stddev /= num_records;
    stddev = sqrt(stddev);
    return aggr;
}
\end{DoxyCode}

\hypertarget{auto__comps_8c_a54e52761faaae64a2040a8c39ac8127c}{\index{auto\-\_\-comps.\-c@{auto\-\_\-comps.\-c}!aggr\-\_\-union\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t@{aggr\-\_\-union\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t}}
\index{aggr\-\_\-union\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t@{aggr\-\_\-union\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t}!auto_comps.c@{auto\-\_\-comps.\-c}}
\subsubsection[{aggr\-\_\-union\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}struct {\bf aggr} {\bf aggr\-\_\-union\-\_\-uint16\-\_\-t} (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{char $\ast$$\ast$}]{records, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{num\-\_\-records, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{field\-\_\-offset}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily  \mbox{[}read\mbox{]}}}}\label{auto__comps_8c_a54e52761faaae64a2040a8c39ac8127c}

\begin{DoxyCode}
{
    struct aggr aggr;
    if (num_records == 0) {
        aggr.num_values = 0;
        aggr.values = NULL;
        return aggr;
    }
    int i;
    uint64_t *temp;
    uint64_t last;
    temp = (uint64_t *)malloc(sizeof(uint64_t)*num_records);
    if (temp == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    for (i=0; i < num_records; i++) {
        temp[i] = *(uint16_t *)(records[i] + field_offset);
    }
    qsort(temp, num_records, sizeof(uint64_t), compar);
    aggr.values = (uint64_t *)malloc(sizeof(uint64_t)*num_records);
    if (aggr.values == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    aggr.values[0] = temp[0];
    last = temp[0];
    aggr.num_values = 1;
    for (i=1; i < num_records; i++) {
        if (temp[i] != last) {
            aggr.values[aggr.num_values++] = temp[i];
            last = temp[i];
        }
    }
    aggr.values = (uint64_t *)realloc(aggr.values, sizeof(uint64_t)*aggr.
      num_values);
    if (aggr.values == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    free(temp);
    return aggr;
}
\end{DoxyCode}

\subsubsection[{aggr\-\_\-union\-\_\-uint64\-\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}struct {\bf aggr} {\bf aggr\-\_\-union\-\_\-uint64\-\_\-t} (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{char $\ast$$\ast$}]{records, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{num\-\_\-records, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{field\-\_\-offset}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily  \mbox{[}read\mbox{]}}}}\label{auto__comps_8c_add8e098cf52612d900fbdbb5c121e0c6}

\begin{DoxyCode}
{
    struct aggr aggr;
    if (num_records == 0) {
        aggr.num_values = 0;
        aggr.values = NULL;
        return aggr;
    }
    int i;
    uint64_t *temp;
    uint64_t last;
    temp = (uint64_t *)malloc(sizeof(uint64_t)*num_records);
    if (temp == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    for (i=0; i < num_records; i++) {
        temp[i] = *(uint64_t *)(records[i] + field_offset);
    }
    qsort(temp, num_records, sizeof(uint64_t), compar);
    aggr.values = (uint64_t *)malloc(sizeof(uint64_t)*num_records);
    if (aggr.values == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    aggr.values[0] = temp[0];
    last = temp[0];
    aggr.num_values = 1;
    for (i=1; i < num_records; i++) {
        if (temp[i] != last) {
            aggr.values[aggr.num_values++] = temp[i];
            last = temp[i];
        }
    }
    aggr.values = (uint64_t *)realloc(aggr.values, sizeof(uint64_t)*aggr.
      num_values);
    if (aggr.values == NULL) {
        perror("malloc");
    }
    free(temp);
    return aggr;
}
\end{DoxyCode}

\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{field\-\_\-offset1, }
\item[{char $\ast$}]{record2, }
\item[{size\-\_\-t}]{field\-\_\-offset2, }

\begin{DoxyCode}

    uint16_t rec2 = *(uint16_t *)(record2 + field_offset2);

\begin{DoxyCode}
{
    if (group1->aggr[field1].num_values == 0 || group2->aggr[field2].num_values
       == 0) {
        return false;
    }
    int i;
    for (i=0; i<group2->aggr[field2].num_values; i++) {
        if (group1->aggr[field1].values[0] >= group2->aggr[field2].values[i] - 
      delta && group1->aggr[field1].values[0] <= group2->aggr[field2].values[i] + 
      delta) {
            return true;
        }
    }
    return false;
}
\end{DoxyCode}
